NOTICE
NO LEGAL RESPONSIBILITY IS ACCEPTED FOR THE PUBLICATION OF ADVERTISEMENTS REGARDING 
CHANGE OF NAME IN THE TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES 
WILL REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER 
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By  Order)
Commissioner  of  Stationery  and  Printing.

PUBLIC NOTICES
	
R. Girish. a male child, son of Thiru V. Raman, born on 20th May 1982, residing at No.11/4, Bharathidasan
2nd Street, Kumaran Colony, Saidapet, Chennai-600 015, has been living as female I have granted Indentity Card No. 2992/09, 
issued by Tamil Nadu Third Gender Welfare Board, Social and NMP Department.  By this, I may be treated as a female and
shall henceforth be known as R. GIRIJA.
R. GIRISH
Chennai, 12th February 2021.
	
T. Prithiviraj, a male child,  son of Thiru S.  Thiyagu, born on 26th May 1992, residing at No. 18, 3rd Street, Gowtham 
Pettai, Tirupattur Taluk, Vellore-635 601.  has been living as female.  I have been granted identity card No. 2637/09 issued 
by Tamil Nadu Third Gender Welfare Board.  Social Welfare and NMP Department By this, I may be treated as female and
shall henceforth be known as ABINAYA. T
T. PRITHIVIRAJ
Vellore, 12th February 2021.
